MODERATE have the seller and the buyer achieved a deal? Yes or No: Because both parties have confirmed the price to be $40. The answer is Yes.

【Before remediation】: 抱歉，$20的价格无法接受，我们的底线价格是每单元$10。【violation】
【Remediation】: 抱歉，$20的价格无法接受，我们的底线价格是每单元$10，希望能够达成双方都能接受的价格。

---- start bargaining ----
  seller: 抱歉，我们公司的底价是每单元$10，无法接受$30的价格。【violation】
  buyer: 你会考虑以每单元$30的价格进行出售吗？
---- start moderating ----
MODERATE have the seller and the buyer achieved a deal? Yes or No: Because the buyer and seller have reached an agreement on the price of $30 per unit and expressed mutual understanding and willingness to work together. The answer is Yes.
